\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ An\ open-\/addressing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ hashtable\ with\ quadratic\ probing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ is\ a\ low\ level\ hashtable\ on\ top\ of\ which\ different\ interfaces\ can\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ implemented,\ like\ flat\_hash\_set,\ node\_hash\_set,\ string\_hash\_set,\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ table\ interface\ is\ similar\ to\ that\ of\ std::unordered\_set.\ Notable}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ differences\ are\ that\ most\ member\ functions\ support\ heterogeneous\ keys\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ BOTH\ the\ hash\ and\ eq\ functions\ are\ marked\ as\ transparent.\ They\ do\ so\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ providing\ a\ typedef\ called\ \`{}is\_transparent`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ When\ heterogeneous\ lookup\ is\ enabled,\ functions\ that\ take\ key\_type\ act\ as\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ they\ have\ an\ overload\ set\ like:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ iterator\ find(const\ key\_type\&\ key);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ template\ <class\ K>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ iterator\ find(const\ K\&\ key);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ size\_type\ erase(const\ key\_type\&\ key);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ template\ <class\ K>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ size\_type\ erase(const\ K\&\ key);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ std::pair<iterator,\ iterator>\ equal\_range(const\ key\_type\&\ key);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ template\ <class\ K>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ std::pair<iterator,\ iterator>\ equal\_range(const\ K\&\ key);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ When\ heterogeneous\ lookup\ is\ disabled,\ only\ the\ explicit\ \`{}key\_type`\ overloads}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ exist.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ find()\ also\ supports\ passing\ the\ hash\ explicitly:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ iterator\ find(const\ key\_type\&\ key,\ size\_t\ hash);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ template\ <class\ U>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ iterator\ find(const\ U\&\ key,\ size\_t\ hash);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ In\ addition\ the\ pointer\ to\ element\ and\ iterator\ stability\ guarantees\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ weaker:\ all\ iterators\ and\ pointers\ are\ invalidated\ after\ a\ new\ element\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ inserted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ IMPLEMENTATION\ DETAILS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \#\ Table\ Layout}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ raw\_hash\_set's\ backing\ array\ consists\ of\ control\ bytes\ followed\ by\ slots}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ that\ may\ or\ may\ not\ contain\ objects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ layout\ of\ the\ backing\ array,\ for\ \`{}capacity`\ slots,\ is\ thus,\ as\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ pseudo-\/struct:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ struct\ BackingArray\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ //\ Sampling\ handler.\ This\ field\ isn't\ present\ when\ the\ sampling\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ //\ disabled\ or\ this\ allocation\ hasn't\ been\ selected\ for\ sampling.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ HashtablezInfoHandle\ infoz\_;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ //\ The\ number\ of\ elements\ we\ can\ insert\ before\ growing\ the\ capacity.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ size\_t\ growth\_left;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ //\ Control\ bytes\ for\ the\ "{}real"{}\ slots.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ ctrl\_t\ ctrl[capacity];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ //\ Always\ \`{}ctrl\_t::kSentinel`.\ This\ is\ used\ by\ iterators\ to\ find\ when\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ //\ stop\ and\ serves\ no\ other\ purpose.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ ctrl\_t\ sentinel;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ //\ A\ copy\ of\ the\ first\ \`{}kWidth\ -\/\ 1`\ elements\ of\ \`{}ctrl`.\ This\ is\ used\ so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ //\ that\ if\ a\ probe\ sequence\ picks\ a\ value\ near\ the\ end\ of\ \`{}ctrl`,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ //\ \`{}Group`\ will\ have\ valid\ control\ bytes\ to\ look\ at.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ ctrl\_t\ clones[kWidth\ -\/\ 1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ //\ The\ actual\ slot\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ slot\_type\ slots[capacity];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \};}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ length\ of\ this\ array\ is\ computed\ by\ \`{}RawHashSetLayout::alloc\_size`\ below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Control\ bytes\ (`ctrl\_t`)\ are\ bytes\ (collected\ into\ groups\ of\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ platform-\/specific\ size)\ that\ define\ the\ state\ of\ the\ corresponding\ slot\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ slot\ array.\ Group\ manipulation\ is\ tightly\ optimized\ to\ be\ as\ efficient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ as\ possible:\ SSE\ and\ friends\ on\ x86,\ clever\ bit\ operations\ on\ other\ arches.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ Group\ 1\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Group\ 2\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Group\ 3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ +-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |\ |}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ +-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Each\ control\ byte\ is\ either\ a\ special\ value\ for\ empty\ slots,\ deleted\ slots}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (sometimes\ called\ *tombstones*),\ and\ a\ special\ end-\/of-\/table\ marker\ used\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ iterators,\ or,\ if\ occupied,\ seven\ bits\ (H2)\ from\ the\ hash\ of\ the\ value\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ corresponding\ slot.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Storing\ control\ bytes\ in\ a\ separate\ array\ also\ has\ beneficial\ cache\ effects,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ since\ more\ logical\ slots\ will\ fit\ into\ a\ cache\ line.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \#\ Small\ Object\ Optimization\ (SOO)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ When\ the\ size/alignment\ of\ the\ value\_type\ and\ the\ capacity\ of\ the\ table\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ small,\ we\ enable\ small\ object\ optimization\ and\ store\ the\ values\ inline\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ raw\_hash\_set\ object.\ This\ optimization\ allows\ us\ to\ avoid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ allocation/deallocation\ as\ well\ as\ cache/dTLB\ misses.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00110\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \#\ Hashing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ compute\ two\ separate\ hashes,\ \`{}H1`\ and\ \`{}H2`,\ from\ the\ hash\ of\ an\ object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}H1(hash(x))`\ is\ an\ index\ into\ \`{}slots`,\ and\ essentially\ the\ starting\ point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ for\ the\ probe\ sequence.\ \`{}H2(hash(x))`\ is\ a\ 7-\/bit\ value\ used\ to\ filter\ out}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00115\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ objects\ that\ cannot\ possibly\ be\ the\ one\ we\ are\ looking\ for.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \#\ Table\ operations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ key\ operations\ are\ \`{}insert`,\ \`{}find`,\ and\ \`{}erase`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Since\ \`{}insert`\ and\ \`{}erase`\ are\ implemented\ in\ terms\ of\ \`{}find`,\ we\ describe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00122\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}find`\ first.\ To\ \`{}find`\ a\ value\ \`{}x`,\ we\ compute\ \`{}hash(x)`.\ From}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00123\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}H1(hash(x))`\ and\ the\ capacity,\ we\ construct\ a\ \`{}probe\_seq`\ that\ visits\ every}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00124\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ group\ of\ slots\ in\ some\ interesting\ order.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00125\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ now\ walk\ through\ these\ indices.\ At\ each\ index,\ we\ select\ the\ entire\ group}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ starting\ with\ that\ index\ and\ extract\ potential\ candidates:\ occupied\ slots}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ with\ a\ control\ byte\ equal\ to\ \`{}H2(hash(x))`.\ If\ we\ find\ an\ empty\ slot\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ group,\ we\ stop\ and\ return\ an\ error.\ Each\ candidate\ slot\ \`{}y`\ is\ compared\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}x`;\ if\ \`{}x\ ==\ y`,\ we\ are\ done\ and\ return\ \`{}\&y`;\ otherwise\ we\ continue\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ next\ probe\ index.\ Tombstones\ effectively\ behave\ like\ full\ slots\ that\ never}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00132\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ match\ the\ value\ we're\ looking\ for.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00133\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00134\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ \`{}H2`\ bits\ ensure\ when\ we\ compare\ a\ slot\ to\ an\ object\ with\ \`{}==`,\ we\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00135\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ likely\ to\ have\ actually\ found\ the\ object.\ \ That\ is,\ the\ chance\ is\ low\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00136\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}==`\ is\ called\ and\ returns\ \`{}false`.\ \ Thus,\ when\ we\ search\ for\ an\ object,\ we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00137\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ are\ unlikely\ to\ call\ \`{}==`\ many\ times.\ \ This\ likelyhood\ can\ be\ analyzed\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00138\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ follows\ (assuming\ that\ H2\ is\ a\ random\ enough\ hash\ function).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00139\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00140\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Let's\ assume\ that\ there\ are\ \`{}k`\ "{}wrong"{}\ objects\ that\ must\ be\ examined\ in\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00141\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ probe\ sequence.\ \ For\ example,\ when\ doing\ a\ \`{}find`\ on\ an\ object\ that\ is\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00142\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ table,\ \`{}k`\ is\ the\ number\ of\ objects\ between\ the\ start\ of\ the\ probe\ sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00143\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ the\ final\ found\ object\ (not\ including\ the\ final\ found\ object).\ \ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00144\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ expected\ number\ of\ objects\ with\ an\ H2\ match\ is\ then\ \`{}k/128`.\ \ Measurements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00145\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ analysis\ indicate\ that\ even\ at\ high\ load\ factors,\ \`{}k`\ is\ less\ than\ 32,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00146\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ meaning\ that\ the\ number\ of\ "{}false\ positive"{}\ comparisons\ we\ must\ perform\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ less\ than\ 1/8\ per\ \`{}find`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}insert`\ is\ implemented\ in\ terms\ of\ \`{}unchecked\_insert`,\ which\ inserts\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ value\ presumed\ to\ not\ be\ in\ the\ table\ (violating\ this\ requirement\ will\ cause}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ table\ to\ behave\ erratically).\ Given\ \`{}x`\ and\ its\ hash\ \`{}hash(x)`,\ to\ insert}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00152\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ it,\ we\ construct\ a\ \`{}probe\_seq`\ once\ again,\ and\ use\ it\ to\ find\ the\ first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00153\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ group\ with\ an\ unoccupied\ (empty\ *or*\ deleted)\ slot.\ We\ place\ \`{}x`\ into\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ first\ such\ slot\ in\ the\ group\ and\ mark\ it\ as\ full\ with\ \`{}x`'s\ H2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00155\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00156\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ To\ \`{}insert`,\ we\ compose\ \`{}unchecked\_insert`\ with\ \`{}find`.\ We\ compute\ \`{}h(x)`\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00157\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ perform\ a\ \`{}find`\ to\ see\ if\ it's\ already\ present;\ if\ it\ is,\ we're\ done.\ If}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00158\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ it's\ not,\ we\ may\ decide\ the\ table\ is\ getting\ overcrowded\ (i.e.\ the\ load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00159\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ factor\ is\ greater\ than\ 7/8\ for\ big\ tables;\ \`{}is\_small()`\ tables\ use\ a\ max\ load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00160\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ factor\ of\ 1);\ in\ this\ case,\ we\ allocate\ a\ bigger\ array,\ \`{}unchecked\_insert`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00161\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ each\ element\ of\ the\ table\ into\ the\ new\ array\ (we\ know\ that\ no\ insertion\ here}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00162\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ will\ insert\ an\ already-\/present\ value),\ and\ discard\ the\ old\ backing\ array.\ At}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00163\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ this\ point,\ we\ may\ \`{}unchecked\_insert`\ the\ value\ \`{}x`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00164\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00165\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Below,\ \`{}unchecked\_insert`\ is\ partly\ implemented\ by\ \`{}prepare\_insert`,\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00166\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ presents\ a\ viable,\ initialized\ slot\ pointee\ to\ the\ caller.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00167\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00168\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}erase`\ is\ implemented\ in\ terms\ of\ \`{}erase\_at`,\ which\ takes\ an\ index\ to\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00169\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ slot.\ Given\ an\ offset,\ we\ simply\ create\ a\ tombstone\ and\ destroy\ its\ contents.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00170\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ If\ we\ can\ prove\ that\ the\ slot\ would\ not\ appear\ in\ a\ probe\ sequence,\ we\ can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00171\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ make\ the\ slot\ as\ empty,\ instead.\ We\ can\ prove\ this\ by\ observing\ that\ if\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00172\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ group\ has\ any\ empty\ slots,\ it\ has\ never\ been\ full\ (assuming\ we\ never\ create}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00173\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ an\ empty\ slot\ in\ a\ group\ with\ no\ empties,\ which\ this\ heuristic\ guarantees\ we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00174\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ never\ do)\ and\ find\ would\ stop\ at\ this\ group\ anyways\ (since\ it\ does\ not\ probe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00175\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ beyond\ groups\ with\ empties).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00176\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00177\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}erase`\ is\ \`{}erase\_at`\ composed\ with\ \`{}find`:\ if\ we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00178\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ have\ a\ value\ \`{}x`,\ we\ can\ perform\ a\ \`{}find`,\ and\ then\ \`{}erase\_at`\ the\ resulting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00179\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ slot.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00180\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00181\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ To\ iterate,\ we\ simply\ traverse\ the\ array,\ skipping\ empty\ and\ deleted\ slots}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00182\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ stopping\ when\ we\ hit\ a\ \`{}kSentinel`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00183\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00309\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ state\ for\ a\ probe\ sequence.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00310\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00311\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Currently,\ the\ sequence\ is\ a\ triangular\ progression\ of\ the\ form}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00312\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00313\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ p(i)\ :=\ Width\ *\ (i\string^2\ +\ i)/2\ +\ hash\ (mod\ mask\ +\ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00314\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00315\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ use\ of\ \`{}Width`\ ensures\ that\ each\ probe\ step\ does\ not\ overlap\ groups;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00316\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ sequence\ effectively\ outputs\ the\ addresses\ of\ *groups*\ (although\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00317\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ necessarily\ aligned\ to\ any\ boundary).\ The\ \`{}Group`\ machinery\ allows\ us}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00318\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ check\ an\ entire\ group\ with\ minimal\ branching.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00319\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00320\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Wrapping\ around\ at\ \`{}mask\ +\ 1`\ is\ important,\ but\ not\ for\ the\ obvious\ reason.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00321\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ As\ described\ above,\ the\ first\ few\ entries\ of\ the\ control\ byte\ array}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00322\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ are\ mirrored\ at\ the\ end\ of\ the\ array,\ which\ \`{}Group`\ will\ find\ and\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00323\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ for\ selecting\ candidates.\ However,\ when\ those\ candidates'\ slots\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00324\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ actually\ inspected,\ there\ are\ no\ corresponding\ slots\ for\ the\ cloned\ bytes,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00325\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ so\ we\ need\ to\ make\ sure\ we've\ treated\ those\ offsets\ as\ "{}wrapping\ around"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00326\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00327\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ It\ turns\ out\ that\ this\ probe\ sequence\ visits\ every\ group\ exactly\ once\ if\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00328\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ number\ of\ groups\ is\ a\ power\ of\ two,\ since\ (i\string^2+i)/2\ is\ a\ bijection\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00329\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Z/(2\string^m).\ See\ https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Quadratic\_probing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00330\ \textcolor{keyword}{template}\ <\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ W\textcolor{keywordtype}{id}th>}
\DoxyCodeLine{00331\ \textcolor{keyword}{class\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classabsl_1_1container__internal_1_1probe__seq}{probe\_seq}}\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{01094\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Stored\ the\ information\ regarding\ number\ of\ slots\ we\ can\ still\ fill}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01095\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ without\ needing\ to\ rehash.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01096\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01097\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ want\ to\ ensure\ sufficient\ number\ of\ empty\ slots\ in\ the\ table\ in\ order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01098\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ keep\ probe\ sequences\ relatively\ short.\ Empty\ slot\ in\ the\ probe\ group}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01099\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ required\ to\ stop\ probing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01100\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01101\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Tombstones\ (kDeleted\ slots)\ are\ not\ included\ in\ the\ growth\ capacity,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01102\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ because\ we'd\ like\ to\ rehash\ when\ the\ table\ is\ filled\ with\ tombstones\ and/or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01103\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ full\ slots.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01104\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03093\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}f`\ must\ abide\ by\ several\ restrictions:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03095\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \`{}raw\_hash\_set::value\_type`\ is\ constructed,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03096\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ it\ MUST\ NOT\ access\ the\ container\ before\ the\ call\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03097\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \`{}raw\_hash\_set::constructor`,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03098\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ it\ MUST\ NOT\ erase\ the\ lazily\ emplaced\ element.}}
